<rating>2</rating>< Review>
The produce here is about what you would find in a grocery store. We saw no evidence that there was any locally grown fruit in the place. The personnel were indifferent to our requests for information and not at all helpful.
The selection is good, though the prices aren't any lower than grocery stores if not a little higher.
If you are on the road passing here, and you want some fruit or vegetables, it is a convenient location. Otherwise, don't go out of your way to visit.<//Review>

<Rate>2< /Rate>< Text>
I had to call multiple Petco stores, none close to either of my locations (west Chula Vista and La Costa/Carlsbad), before I found one that actually had a few crickets left to sell me to feed my son's starving fire belly toad (I had been trying for days at a time in Chula Vista). I was charged $0.16 each for ten medium crickets.There was tax added. I am very expert in caring for animals (the tablespoon-size toad is 16 years old) and I know how to keep a clean cricket keeper with calcium cubes, a cap of water, spinach or fresh potato, etc. A good batch of crickets will live 10 days or more. These crickets died in the keeper, all but three (one the toad ate the first day, another two days later, and the last alive one yesterday) survived for me to feed the toad. I watch the feeding and 'rescue' the crickets if they get caught in the water side before they drown. This was a bad batch of crickets that I went out of my way to buy. Since crickets are so fragile, and often at the end of their lifespans, it should be customary to provide the customer with several extra crickets at no charge. I now have to buy more crickets just four days later. It is both inconvenient and expensive. The crickets died because they were 'old', no other explanation. I pay too much for crickets that are ready to die. Unlike PetsMart, Petco charges the SAME PRICE for crickets of any size, which is not fair. A large cricket is equal in total mass to two medium crickets. But, I had to buy what was available. The medium are a bit small but the large ones sometimes are too big for the toad's mouth.</Text>

This company has the worst customer service I’ve ever dealt with. Every time I call, I’ve had to wait at least 15 to 20 minutes or longer to talk to someone. And each time, the person tells me that they’re putting a “note” in my file about what they took care of for me. I’ve also had to call them back multiple times myself because I never get a return call like I’m promised.
Also, I was told I would get free service for a year with a purchase of a softener and a filter that was ~$4,000. Then they just started charging me out of nowhere two different times. When I called to ask them why I was being charged, they act like they have no idea what’s going on. And I have to make multiple phone calls to get the issue taken care of.
They are obviously very disorganized and do not follow through with what they say they’re going to do. I would not recommend this company.< /Review>

< text>
Careful.. This place has gone through ownership and does not have the same menu anymore. Starters are down to fried food and the regular menu has changed as well. No more happy hour. We tried the sweet fries , which was just a handful, Korean chili cheese chicken bites (decent),  house Tatar tots (not so good) and pasta with chicken which reminded me of my Lean Cuisine lunch. Place is empty on a Thursday evening. The layout is not really comfortable, as they are adding a bar. Given the fact that the staff was friendly and service really good, I think 3 stars are appropriate. Might be back, if they add a happy hour.</text>

Service: 5/5

My server Ellen did such an amazing job at recommending certain dishes and was super honest about which ones she favors. She was extremely attentive and was always checking up if we needed anything. Food came out SUPER fast, was hot, and very delicious!

Food: 5/5

Japanese Miso Burger - By far my favorite thing to eat was the Japanese Miso Burger. Didn't expect it to be as great as it sounded, but it was so delicious, I'm still craving it today!

Kimchi Fried Rice and Kimchi Penne Pasta - I also got the Kimchi Fried Rice and Kimchi Penne Pasta which both were delicious to try! Just be careful if you're not a spicy food kind of person.

Fried Calamari - Battered perfectly, and crispy as it should be! The sauce they use wasn't a normal tartar sauce, but it still tasted amazing.

Chili Cheese Fries - ok I'm not gonna lie, I thought they were going to be some random fries thrown together with some meat on top. But I was totally wrong! It came with crispy, crunchy fries, a deliciously spicy and sweet sauce on top, and a beautiful sunny side up egg that left a runny BEAUTIFUL yolk that spilled across the fries. Honestly - a picture perfect opp or boomerang for any Instagram lovers.

Pricing 5/5

You. Get. What. You. Pay. For. It was reasonably priced with the perfect amount of food to share with the entire party.

Honestly, I would definitely recommend anyone who has a birthday or even a celebratory event coming up because this place was able to accommodate my large party of 8! Would definitely come back soon. <Review>Overall experiences with Jersey Mikes have been good, but today I realized the confusion that comes to the employees when making pickup orders. < review>
As a parent of a team gymnast, I can not say enough good things about Airborne after experiencing 2 other competing gyms in the area. Airborne and its team coaches are dedicated to the girls and their success. The feedback my daughter receives while being coached is always done in a positive manner. Through Covid, Airborne did everything they possibly could under the County guidelines to continue the team’s training and we are forever grateful. Parents can observe practices through Spot TV. The facility is regularly sanitized and exceptionally clean with health and safety being top priority at the gym. Airborne is our daughter’s “happy place”. She loves gymnastics and Airborne is the perfect fit for her and our family.</review>

When the representative arrived, he said it would be $180.00.The hallway was approximately 3 x 8’ and the living room was a normal sized “room”. He would only do the small hallway and the small traffic area in the living room (approximately the same sized area as above hallway) for the $104.00. He would not do the room. My parents added a deodorizer for the hallway so the total cost was $124.00.  Had he cleaned the living room as requested and reflected as a part of the price, the total would have been something in the area of $240.00. This included the added deodorizer. We did not get the “room” cleaned as desired. Many spots remain and the rep was a bit difficult with the nursing aide that questioned him on the total amount and the area to be cleaned.
We felt misled, to be honest.  We were happy with the cleaning result in the hallway, but the cleaning rep was unaccomodating and we felt that we will use someone else in the future.
Thanks.</Text>
